Abstract\nThe\nobjective\nof\nthis\ninvestigation\nis\nto\ndevelop\na technology.base\nfor\nthe\nthermal\nacoustic\nshield\nconcept\nas\na noise\nsuppression\ndevice\nfor\nslngie\nstream\nexhaust\nnozzles.\nAcoustic\ndata\nfor\n314\ntest\npoints\nfor\n9 scale\nmodel\nnozzle\nconfigurations\nwere\nobtained.\nFive\nof\nthese\nconfigurations\nemployed\nan unsuppressed\nannular\nplug\ncore\njet\nand\nthe\nremaining\nfour\nnozzles\nemployed\na 32 chute\nsuppressor\ncore\nnozzle.\nInfluence\nof\nsimulated\nflight\nand\nselected\ngeometric\nand\naerodynamic\nflow\nvariables\non the\nacoustic\nbehavior\nof\nthe\nthermal\nacoustic\nshield\nwas\ndetermined.\nLaser\nvelocimeter\nand\naerodynamic\nmeasurements\nwere\nemployed\nto\nyield\nvaluable\ndiagnostic\ninformation\nregarding\nthe\nflow\nfield\ncharacteristics\nof\nthese\nnozzles.\nAn existing\ntheoretical\naeroacoustic\nprediction\nmethod\nwas\nmodified\nto\npredict\nthe\nacoustic\ncharacteristics\nof\npartial\nthermal\nacoustic\nshields.\nFrom\nthe\nresults\nof\nthis\ninvestigation,\nit\nwas\nfound\nthat:\nthe\nthree\nsignificant\nphysical\ninfluences\nof\na\nthermal\nacoustic\nshield\nare:\nI)\nmid\nand\nhigh\nfrequency\nnoise\nreduction\nat\nshallow\nan_les\nto\nthe\njet\naxis\ndue\nto\ntotal\ninternal\nreflection;\n2)\nmid\nand\nhigh\nfrequency\nnolse\nreduction\nin\nthe\nfront\nquadrant\nand\nat\ne 1 : 90 \xc2\xb0 due\nto\nsource\nstrength\nreduction;\nand 3)\nlow\nfrequency\nnoise\namplification\ndue\nto\nan elongation\nof\nthe\njet\nplume.\nDue\nto\nthe\nlarger\nhigh\nfrequency\nnoise\ncontent\nof\nthe\n32 chute\nsuppressor\nnozzle,\nthe\nthermal\nacoustic\nshield\nyields\nlarger\nPNL\nand\nEPNL\nreductions\ndue\nto\nthe\nthermal\nacoustic\nshield\nare\ndependent\non the\nobserver\nsideline\ndistance,\nand\nhence\nappropriate\nsideline\ndistances\nmust\nbe\nutilized\nin\ndetermining\nthe\nnoise\nsuppression\nat\ntakeoff,\ncutback\nand\napproach\ncycle\nconditions.\nThe\nshield\nthickness\nhas\na significant\nbearing\non the\nnoise\nreduction\npotential\nof\na thermal\nacoustic\nshield.\nPartial\nthermal\nacoustic\nshields\ncreate\nsignificant\namount\nof acoustic\nand\nflow\nasymmetry\nwhich\nis confirmed\nby the\ntheoretical\npredictions.\nAn\nincrease\nin\nbase\ndrag\nof the 32 chute\nsuppressor\nnozzle\ndue\nto
